# Items Master List Addendum — DepthPack MEGA (IDs 30000–32999)

Generated baseline expansion: Common/Uncommon/Rare focus.

## Frostbit Warrant (ID: 30000)
- **Category:** Document / Map Fragment
- **Rarity:** Uncommon
- **Region:** Glimmerdeep
- **Professions:** None
- **Short Summary:** Glimmerdeep map fragment document: traded at night markets, often a quest turn-in.
- **Icon:** `document_frostbit_warrant.png`
